     1	namespace Spectre.Console;
     2	
     3	/// <summary>
     4	/// Represents a prompt.
     5	/// </summary>
     6	/// <typeparam name="T">The prompt result type.</typeparam>
     7	public sealed class TextPrompt<T> : IPrompt<T>, IHasCulture
     8	{
     9	    private readonly string _prompt;
    10	    private readonly StringComparer? _comparer;
    11	
    12	    /// <summary>
    13	    /// Gets or sets the prompt style.
    14	    /// </summary>
    15	    public Style? PromptStyle { get; set; }
    16	
    17	    /// <summary>
    18	    /// Gets the list of choices.
    19	    /// </summary>
    20	    public List<T> Choices { get; } = [];
    21	
    22	    /// <summary>
    23	    /// Gets or sets the culture to use when converting input to object.
    24	    /// </summary>
    25	    public CultureInfo? Culture { get; set; }
    26	
    27	    /// <summary>
    28	    /// Gets or sets the message for invalid choices.
    29	    /// </summary>
    30	    public string InvalidChoiceMessage { get; set; } = "[red]Please select one of the available options[/]";
    31	
    32	    /// <summary>
    33	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether input should
    34	    /// be hidden in the console.
    35	    /// </summary>
    36	    public bool IsSecret { get; set; }
    37	
    38	    /// <summary>
    39	    /// Gets or sets the character to use while masking
    40	    /// a secret prompt.
    41	    /// </summary>
    42	    public char? Mask { get; set; } = '*';
    43	
    44	    /// <summary>
    45	    /// Gets or sets the validation error message.
    46	    /// </summary>
    47	    public string ValidationErrorMessage { get; set; } = "[red]Invalid input[/]";
    48	
    49	    /// <summary>
    50	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether or not
    51	    /// choices should be shown.
    52	    /// </summary>
    53	    public bool ShowChoices { get; set; } = true;
    54	
    55	    /// <summary>
    56	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether or not
    57	    /// default values should be shown.
    58	    /// </summary>
    59	    public bool ShowDefaultValue { get; set; } = true;
    60	
    61	    /// <summary>
    62	    /// Gets or sets the default value editable state that allows the injection of the DefaultValue in the text field.
    63	    /// If true this places the DefaultValue in the input buffer which can then be edited by the user.
    64	    /// </summary>
    65	    public bool EditableDefaultValue { get; set; }
    66	
    67	    /// <summary>
    68	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether or not an empty result is valid.
    69	    /// </summary>
    70	    public bool AllowEmpty { get; set; }
    71	
    72	    /// <summary>
    73	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether the prompt line
    74	    /// should be cleared after a successful input.
    75	    /// </summary>
    76	    public bool ClearOnFinish { get; set; }
    77	
    78	    /// <summary>
    79	    /// Gets or sets the converter to get the display string for a choice. By default
    80	    /// the corresponding <see cref="TypeConverter"/> is used.
    81	    /// </summary>
    82	    public Func<T, string>? Converter { get; set; } = TypeConverterHelper.ConvertToString;
    83	
    84	    /// <summary>
    85	    /// Gets or sets the validator.
    86	    /// </summary>
    87	    public Func<T, ValidationResult>? Validator { get; set; }
    88	
    89	    /// <summary>
    90	    /// Gets or sets the style in which the default value is displayed. Defaults to green when <see langword="null"/>.
    91	    /// </summary>
    92	    public Style? DefaultValueStyle { get; set; }
    93	
    94	    /// <summary>
    95	    /// Gets or sets the style in which the list of choices is displayed. Defaults to blue when <see langword="null"/>.
    96	    /// </summary>
    97	    public Style? ChoicesStyle { get; set; }
    98	
    99	    /// <summary>
   100	    /// Gets or sets the default value.
   101	    /// </summary>
   102	    internal DefaultPromptValue<T>? DefaultValue { get; set; }
   103	
   104	    /// <summary>
   105	    /// Initializes a new instance of the <see cref="TextPrompt{T}"/> class.
   106	    /// </summary>
   107	    /// <param name="prompt">The prompt markup text.</param>
   108	    /// <param name="comparer">The comparer used for choices.</param>
   109	    public TextPrompt(string prompt, StringComparer? comparer = null)
   110	    {
   111	        _prompt = prompt ?? throw new System.ArgumentNullException(nameof(prompt));
   112	        _comparer = comparer;
   113	    }
   114	
   115	    /// <summary>
   116	    /// Shows the prompt and requests input from the user.
   117	    /// </summary>
   118	    /// <param name="console">The console to show the prompt in.</param>
   119	    /// <returns>The user input converted to the expected type.</returns>
   120	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   121	    public T Show(IAnsiConsole console)
   122	    {
   123	        return ShowAsync(console, CancellationToken.None).GetAwaiter().GetResult();
   124	    }
   125	
   126	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   127	    public async Task<T> ShowAsync(IAnsiConsole console, CancellationToken cancellationToken)
   128	    {
   129	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(console);
   130	
   131	        return await console.RunExclusive(async () =>
   132	        {
   133	            var promptStyle = PromptStyle ?? Style.Plain;
   134	            var converter = Converter ?? TypeConverterHelper.ConvertToString;
   135	            var choices = Choices.Select(choice => converter(choice)).ToList();
   136	            var choiceMap = Choices.ToDictionary(choice => converter(choice), choice => choice, _comparer);
   137	
   138	            WritePrompt(console);
   139	
   140	            while (true)
   141	            {
   142	                string input;
   143	                if (EditableDefaultValue && DefaultValue != null)
   144	                {
   145	                    input = await console.ReadLine(promptStyle, IsSecret, Mask, choices, cancellationToken, converter(DefaultValue.Value)).ConfigureAwait(false);
   146	                }
   147	                else
   148	                {
   149	                    input = await console.ReadLine(promptStyle, IsSecret, Mask, choices, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);
   150	                }
   151	
   152	
   153	
   154	                // Nothing entered?
   155	                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(input))
   156	                {
   157	                    if (DefaultValue != null)
   158	                    {
   159	                        var defaultValue = converter(DefaultValue.Value);
   160	                        console.Write(IsSecret ? defaultValue.Mask(Mask) : defaultValue, promptStyle);
   161	                        console.WriteLine();
   162	
   163	                        ClearPromptLine(console);
   164	                        return DefaultValue.Value;
   165	                    }
   166	
   167	                    if (!AllowEmpty)
   168	                    {
   169	                        continue;
   170	                    }
   171	                }
   172	
   173	                console.WriteLine();
   174	
   175	                T? result;
   176	                if (Choices.Count > 0)
   177	                {
   178	                    if (choiceMap.TryGetValue(input, out result) && result != null)
   179	                    {
   180	                        ClearPromptLine(console);
   181	                        return result;
   182	                    }
   183	                    else
   184	                    {
   185	                        console.MarkupLine(InvalidChoiceMessage);
   186	                        WritePrompt(console);
   187	                        continue;
   188	                    }
   189	                }
   190	                else if (!TypeConverterHelper.TryConvertFromStringWithCulture<T>(input, Culture, out result) || result == null)
   191	                {
   192	                    console.MarkupLine(ValidationErrorMessage);
   193	                    WritePrompt(console);
   194	                    continue;
   195	                }
   196	
   197	                // Run all validators
   198	                if (!ValidateResult(result, out var validationMessage))
   199	                {
   200	                    console.MarkupLine(validationMessage);
   201	                    WritePrompt(console);
   202	                    continue;
   203	                }
   204	
   205	                ClearPromptLine(console);
   206	                return result;
   207	            }
   208	        }).ConfigureAwait(false);
   209	    }
   210	
   211	    /// <summary>
   212	    /// Writes the prompt to the console.
   213	    /// </summary>
   214	    /// <param name="console">The console to write the prompt to.</param>
   215	    private void WritePrompt(IAnsiConsole console)
   216	    {
   217	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(console);
   218	
   219	        var builder = new StringBuilder();
   220	        builder.Append(_prompt.TrimEnd());
   221	
   222	        var appendSuffix = false;
   223	        if (ShowChoices && Choices.Count > 0)
   224	        {
   225	            appendSuffix = true;
   226	            var converter = Converter ?? TypeConverterHelper.ConvertToString;
   227	            var choices = string.Join("/", Choices.Select(choice => converter(choice)));
   228	            var choicesStyle = ChoicesStyle?.ToMarkup() ?? "blue";
   229	            builder.AppendFormat(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, " [{0}][[{1}]][/]", choicesStyle, choices);
   230	        }
   231	
   232	        if (ShowDefaultValue && DefaultValue != null)
   233	        {
   234	            appendSuffix = true;
   235	            var converter = Converter ?? TypeConverterHelper.ConvertToString;
   236	            var defaultValueStyle = DefaultValueStyle?.ToMarkup() ?? "green";
   237	            var defaultValue = converter(DefaultValue.Value);
   238	
   239	            builder.AppendFormat(
   240	                CultureInfo.InvariantCulture,
   241	                " [{0}]({1})[/]",
   242	                defaultValueStyle,
   243	                IsSecret ? defaultValue.Mask(Mask) : defaultValue);
   244	        }
   245	
   246	        var markup = builder.ToString().Trim();
   247	        if (appendSuffix)
   248	        {
   249	            markup += ":";
   250	        }
   251	
   252	        console.Markup(markup + " ");
   253	    }
   254	
   255	    /// <summary>
   256	    /// Clears the prompt line when enabled.
   257	    /// </summary>
   258	    /// <param name="console">The console to clear the prompt from.</param>
   259	    private void ClearPromptLine(IAnsiConsole console)
   260	    {
   261	        if (!ClearOnFinish)
   262	        {
   263	            return;
   264	        }
   265	
   266	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(console);
   267	
   268	        if (!console.Profile.Capabilities.Ansi)
   269	        {
   270	            return;
   271	        }
   272	
   273	        console.Cursor.MoveUp();
   274	        console.Write(ControlCode.Create(console, writer =>
   275	        {
   276	            writer.Write("\r");
   277	            writer.EraseInLine(2);
   278	        }));
   279	    }
   280	
   281	    private bool ValidateResult(T value, [NotNullWhen(false)] out string? message)
   282	    {
   283	        if (Validator != null)
   284	        {
   285	            var result = Validator(value);
   286	            if (!result.Successful)
   287	            {
   288	                message = result.Message ?? ValidationErrorMessage;
   289	                return false;
   290	            }
   291	        }
   292	
   293	        message = null;
   294	        return true;
   295	    }
   296	}

     3	/// <summary>
     4	/// Contains extension methods for <see cref="TextPrompt{T}"/>.
     5	/// </summary>
     6	public static class TextPromptExtensions
     7	{
     8	    /// <summary>
     9	    /// Allow empty input.
    10	    /// </summary>
    11	    /// <typeparam name="T">The prompt result type.</typeparam>
    12	    /// <param name="obj">The prompt.</param>
    13	    /// <returns>The same instance so that multiple calls can be chained.</returns>
    14	    public static TextPrompt<T> AllowEmpty<T>(this TextPrompt<T> obj)
    15	    {
    16	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(obj);
    17	
    18	        obj.AllowEmpty = true;
    19	        return obj;
    20	    }
    21	
    22	    /// <summary>
    23	    /// Sets the prompt style.
    24	    /// </summary>
    25	    /// <typeparam name="T">The prompt result type.</typeparam>
    26	    /// <param name="obj">The prompt.</param>
    27	    /// <param name="style">The prompt style.</param>
    28	    /// <returns>The same instance so that multiple calls can be chained.</returns>
    29	    public static TextPrompt<T> PromptStyle<T>(this TextPrompt<T> obj, Style style)
    30	    {
    31	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(obj);
    32	
    33	        obj.PromptStyle = style;
    34	        return obj;
    35	    }

    37	    /// <summary>
    38	    /// Show or hide choices.

    43	    /// <returns>The same instance so that multiple calls can be chained.</returns>
    44	    public static TextPrompt<T> ShowChoices<T>(this TextPrompt<T> obj, bool show)
    45	    {
    46	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(obj);
    47	
    48	        obj.ShowChoices = show;
    49	        return obj;
    50	    }
    51	
    52	    /// <summary>
    53	    /// Shows choices.
    54	    /// </summary>
    55	    /// <typeparam name="T">The prompt result type.</typeparam>
    56	    /// <param name="obj">The prompt.</param>
    57	    /// <returns>The same instance so that multiple calls can be chained.</returns>

   176	    /// <param name="message">The validation error message.</param>
   177	    /// <returns>The same instance so that multiple calls can be chained.</returns>
   178	    public static TextPrompt<T> Validate<T>(this TextPrompt<T> obj, Func<T, bool> validator, string? message = null)
   179	    {
   180	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(obj);
   181	
   182	        obj.Validator = result =>
   183	        {
   184	            if (validator(result))
   185	            {
   186	                return ValidationResult.Success();
   187	            }
   188	
   189	            return ValidationResult.Error(message);
   190	        };
   191	
   192	        return obj;
   193	    }

Now I understand the issue. Looking at the `TextPrompt.cs` code, I can see:

1. Line 108-113: The constructor takes an optional `StringComparer? comparer` parameter.
2. Line 136: `var choiceMap = Choices.ToDictionary(choice => converter(choice), choice => choice, _comparer);`

The `_comparer` is used when building the dictionary to compare choices. However, the issue is that even if someone passes a case-insensitive comparer, the `_comparer` defaults to `null` (which means `EqualityComparer<string>.Default`, which is case-sensitive).

The PR wants to make `TextPrompt<string>` case-insensitive by default when comparing choices. 

Let me also check if there's a way to pass the comparer currently:

The constructor already accepts a `StringComparer?`. But looking at the PR description, the user creates `new TextPrompt<string>("...")` and adds choices - they want it to be case-insensitive by default.

     3	/// <summary>
     4	/// A prompt that is answered with a yes or no.
     5	/// </summary>
     6	public sealed class ConfirmationPrompt : IPrompt<bool>
     7	{
     8	    private readonly string _prompt;
     9	
    10	    /// <summary>
    11	    /// Gets or sets the character that represents "yes".
    12	    /// </summary>
    13	    public char Yes { get; set; } = 'y';
    14	
    15	    /// <summary>
    16	    /// Gets or sets the character that represents "no".
    17	    /// </summary>
    18	    public char No { get; set; } = 'n';
    19	
    20	    /// <summary>
    21	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether "yes" is the default answer.
    22	    /// </summary>
    23	    public bool DefaultValue { get; set; } = true;
    24	
    25	    /// <summary>
    26	    /// Gets or sets the message for invalid choices.
    27	    /// </summary>
    28	    public string InvalidChoiceMessage { get; set; } = "[red]Please select one of the available options[/]";
    29	
    30	    /// <summary>
    31	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether or not
    32	    /// choices should be shown.
    33	    /// </summary>
    34	    public bool ShowChoices { get; set; } = true;
    35	
    36	    /// <summary>
    37	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether or not
    38	    /// default values should be shown.
    39	    /// </summary>
    40	    public bool ShowDefaultValue { get; set; } = true;
    41	
    42	    /// <summary>
    43	    /// Gets or sets the style in which the default value is displayed. Defaults to green when <see langword="null"/>.
    44	    /// </summary>
    45	    public Style? DefaultValueStyle { get; set; }
    46	
    47	    /// <summary>
    48	    /// Gets or sets the style in which the list of choices is displayed. Defaults to blue when <see langword="null"/>.
    49	    /// </summary>
    50	    public Style? ChoicesStyle { get; set; }
    51	
    52	    /// <summary>
    53	    /// Gets or sets the string comparer to use when comparing user input
    54	    /// against Yes/No choices.
    55	    /// </summary>
    56	    /// <remarks>
    57	    /// Defaults to <see cref="StringComparer.CurrentCultureIgnoreCase"/>.
    58	    /// </remarks>
    59	    public StringComparer Comparer { get; set; } = StringComparer.CurrentCultureIgnoreCase;
    60	
    61	    /// <summary>
    62	    /// Initializes a new instance of the <see cref="ConfirmationPrompt"/> class.
    63	    /// </summary>
    64	    /// <param name="prompt">The prompt markup text.</param>
    65	    public ConfirmationPrompt(string prompt)
    66	    {
    67	        _prompt = prompt ?? throw new System.ArgumentNullException(nameof(prompt));
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    71	    public bool Show(IAnsiConsole console)
    72	    {
    73	        return ShowAsync(console, CancellationToken.None).GetAwaiter().GetResult();
    74	    }
    75	
    76	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    77	    public async Task<bool> ShowAsync(IAnsiConsole console, CancellationToken cancellationToken)
    78	    {
    79	        var comparer = Comparer ?? StringComparer.CurrentCultureIgnoreCase;
    80	
    81	        var prompt = new TextPrompt<char>(_prompt, comparer)
    82	            .InvalidChoiceMessage(InvalidChoiceMessage)
    83	            .ValidationErrorMessage(InvalidChoiceMessage)
    84	            .ShowChoices(ShowChoices)
    85	            .ChoicesStyle(ChoicesStyle)
    86	            .ShowDefaultValue(ShowDefaultValue)
    87	            .DefaultValue(DefaultValue ? Yes : No)
    88	            .DefaultValueStyle(DefaultValueStyle)
    89	            .AddChoice(Yes)
    90	            .AddChoice(No);
    91	
    92	        var result = await prompt.ShowAsync(console, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);
    93	
    94	        return comparer.Compare(Yes.ToString(), result.ToString()) == 0;
    95	    }
    96	}

Now I see the pattern clearly. The `ConfirmationPrompt` already has a `Comparer` property that defaults to `StringComparer.CurrentCultureIgnoreCase`. But `TextPrompt<T>` only accepts a comparer in the constructor and defaults to `null` (case-sensitive).

The fix should be:
1. Add a `Comparer` property to `TextPrompt<T>` (like `ConfirmationPrompt` has) that defaults to `StringComparer.CurrentCultureIgnoreCase`
2. Use that property in the choice dictionary creation and in the comparison logic

But wait - `TextPrompt<T>` is generic. For non-string types, a `StringComparer` doesn't make sense. Let me think about this more carefully.

Looking at the code again, the `_comparer` field is used specifically for comparing the string representation of choices (via `converter`). So it's really about comparing the string keys in the dictionary `choiceMap`. 

The PR description specifically asks for `TextPrompt<string>` to be case-insensitive. Looking at the constructor, it already accepts a `StringComparer?` parameter. The problem is that when you use `new TextPrompt<string>("...")`, the default is `null`, which means case-sensitive comparison.

The simplest fix is to add a property like `ConfirmationPrompt` has and make the existing constructor use it properly. But we need to maintain backward compatibility.

Let me check if there are tests that rely on case-sensitive behavior:

Looking at the test file, I don't see tests specifically testing case sensitivity. Let me look for any existing expectations related to this.

Now I understand the full picture. Let me make the changes to `TextPrompt.cs`:

The key changes needed:
1. Add a `Comparer` property (like `ConfirmationPrompt`) that defaults to `StringComparer.CurrentCultureIgnoreCase`
2. In `ShowAsync`, use `_comparer ?? Comparer` (or just `_comparer ?? StringComparer.CurrentCultureIgnoreCase`) when creating the dictionary

Actually, looking at the code more carefully, the constructor already stores `_comparer`. The issue is that it defaults to `null`. The simplest and most consistent fix is to add a property `Comparer` and use it when `_comparer` is null.

   109	    public TextPrompt(string prompt, StringComparer? comparer = null)
   110	    {

   112	        _comparer = comparer;
   113	    }
   114	
   115	    /// <summary>
   116	    /// Shows the prompt and requests input from the user.
   117	    /// </summary>
   118	    /// <param name="console">The console to show the prompt in.</param>
   119	    /// <returns>The user input converted to the expected type.</returns>
   120	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   121	    public T Show(IAnsiConsole console)
   122	    {
   123	        return ShowAsync(console, CancellationToken.None).GetAwaiter().GetResult();
   124	    }
   125	
   126	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   127	    public async Task<T> ShowAsync(IAnsiConsole console, CancellationToken cancellationToken)
   128	    {
   129	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(console);
   130	
   131	        return await console.RunExclusive(async () =>
   132	        {
   133	            var promptStyle = PromptStyle ?? Style.Plain;
   134	            var converter = Converter ?? TypeConverterHelper.ConvertToString;
   135	            var choices = Choices.Select(choice => converter(choice)).ToList();
   136	            var choiceMap = Choices.ToDictionary(choice => converter(choice), choice => choice, _comparer);
   137	
   138	            WritePrompt(console);
   139	
   140	            while (true)
   141	            {
   142	                string input;
   143	                if (EditableDefaultValue && DefaultValue != null)
   144	                {
   145	                    input = await console.ReadLine(promptStyle, IsSecret, Mask, choices, cancellationToken, converter(DefaultValue.Value)).ConfigureAwait(false);
   146	                }
   147	                else
   148	                {
   149	                    input = await console.ReadLine(promptStyle, IsSecret, Mask, choices, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);
   150	                }
   151	
   152	
   153	
   154	                // Nothing entered?
   155	                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(input))
   156	                {
   157	                    if (DefaultValue != null)
   158	                    {
   159	                        var defaultValue = converter(DefaultValue.Value);
   160	                        console.Write(IsSecret ? defaultValue.Mask(Mask) : defaultValue, promptStyle);
   161	                        console.WriteLine();
   162	
   163	                        ClearPromptLine(console);
   164	                        return DefaultValue.Value;
   165	                    }
   166	
   167	                    if (!AllowEmpty)
   168	                    {
   169	                        continue;
   170	                    }
   171	                }
   172	
   173	                console.WriteLine();
   174	
   175	                T? result;
   176	                if (Choices.Count > 0)
   177	                {
   178	                    if (choiceMap.TryGetValue(input, out result) && result != null)
   179	                    {
   180	                        ClearPromptLine(console);
   181	                        return result;
   182	                    }
   183	                    else
   184	                    {
   185	                        console.MarkupLine(InvalidChoiceMessage);
   186	                        WritePrompt(console);
   187	                        continue;
   188	                    }
   189	                }
   190	                else if (!TypeConverterHelper.TryConvertFromStringWithCulture<T>(input, Culture, out result) || result == null)
   191	                {
   192	                    console.MarkupLine(ValidationErrorMessage);
   193	                    WritePrompt(console);
   194	                    continue;
   195	                }
   196	
   197	                // Run all validators
   198	                if (!ValidateResult(result, out var validationMessage))
   199	                {
   200	                    console.MarkupLine(validationMessage);
   201	                    WritePrompt(console);
   202	                    continue;
   203	                }
   204	
   205	                ClearPromptLine(console);
   206	                return result;
   207	            }
   208	        }).ConfigureAwait(false);
   209	    }
   210	
   211	    /// <summary>
   212	    /// Writes the prompt to the console.
   213	    /// </summary>
   214	    /// <param name="console">The console to write the prompt to.</param>
   215	    private void WritePrompt(IAnsiConsole console)
   216	    {
   217	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(console);
   218	
   219	        var builder = new StringBuilder();
   220	        builder.Append(_prompt.TrimEnd());
   221	
   222	        var appendSuffix = false;
   223	        if (ShowChoices && Choices.Count > 0)
   224	        {
   225	            appendSuffix = true;
   226	            var converter = Converter ?? TypeConverterHelper.ConvertToString;
   227	            var choices = string.Join("/", Choices.Select(choice => converter(choice)));
   228	            var choicesStyle = ChoicesStyle?.ToMarkup() ?? "blue";
   229	            builder.AppendFormat(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, " [{0}][[{1}]][/]", choicesStyle, choices);
   230	        }
   231	
   232	        if (ShowDefaultValue && DefaultValue != null)
   233	        {
   234	            appendSuffix = true;
   235	            var converter = Converter ?? TypeConverterHelper.ConvertToString;
   236	            var defaultValueStyle = DefaultValueStyle?.ToMarkup() ?? "green";
   237	            var defaultValue = converter(DefaultValue.Value);
   238	
   239	            builder.AppendFormat(
   240	                CultureInfo.InvariantCulture,
   241	                " [{0}]({1})[/]",
   242	                defaultValueStyle,
   243	                IsSecret ? defaultValue.Mask(Mask) : defaultValue);
   244	        }
   245	
   246	        var markup = builder.ToString().Trim();
   247	        if (appendSuffix)
   248	        {
   249	            markup += ":";
   250	        }
   251	
   252	        console.Markup(markup + " ");
   253	    }
   254	
   255	    /// <summary>
   256	    /// Clears the prompt line when enabled.
   257	    /// </summary>
   258	    /// <param name="console">The console to clear the prompt from.</param>
   259	    private void ClearPromptLine(IAnsiConsole console)
   260	    {
   261	        if (!ClearOnFinish)
   262	        {
   263	            return;
   264	        }
   265	
   266	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(console);
   267	
   268	        if (!console.Profile.Capabilities.Ansi)
   269	        {
   270	            return;
   271	        }
   272	
   273	        console.Cursor.MoveUp();
   274	        console.Write(ControlCode.Create(console, writer =>
   275	        {
   276	            writer.Write("\r");
   277	            writer.EraseInLine(2);
   278	        }));
   279	    }
   280	
   281	    private bool ValidateResult(T value, [NotNullWhen(false)] out string? message)
   282	    {
   283	        if (Validator != null)
   284	        {
   285	            var result = Validator(value);
   286	            if (!result.Successful)
   287	            {
   288	                message = result.Message ?? ValidationErrorMessage;

     1	namespace Spectre.Console;
     2	
     3	/// <summary>
     4	/// Represents a prompt.
     5	/// </summary>
     6	/// <typeparam name="T">The prompt result type.</typeparam>
     7	public sealed class TextPrompt<T> : IPrompt<T>, IHasCulture
     8	{
     9	    private readonly string _prompt;
    10	    private readonly StringComparer? _comparer;
    11	
    12	    /// <summary>
    13	    /// Gets or sets the prompt style.
    14	    /// </summary>
    15	    public Style? PromptStyle { get; set; }
    16	
    17	    /// <summary>
    18	    /// Gets the list of choices.
    19	    /// </summary>
    20	    public List<T> Choices { get; } = [];
    21	
    22	    /// <summary>
    23	    /// Gets or sets the culture to use when converting input to object.
    24	    /// </summary>
    25	    public CultureInfo? Culture { get; set; }
    26	
    27	    /// <summary>
    28	    /// Gets or sets the message for invalid choices.
    29	    /// </summary>
    30	    public string InvalidChoiceMessage { get; set; } = "[red]Please select one of the available options[/]";
    31	
    32	    /// <summary>
    33	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether input should
    34	    /// be hidden in the console.
    35	    /// </summary>
    36	    public bool IsSecret { get; set; }
    37	
    38	    /// <summary>
    39	    /// Gets or sets the character to use while masking
    40	    /// a secret prompt.
    41	    /// </summary>
    42	    public char? Mask { get; set; } = '*';
    43	
    44	    /// <summary>
    45	    /// Gets or sets the validation error message.
    46	    /// </summary>
    47	    public string ValidationErrorMessage { get; set; } = "[red]Invalid input[/]";
    48	
    49	    /// <summary>
    50	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether or not
    51	    /// choices should be shown.
    52	    /// </summary>
    53	    public bool ShowChoices { get; set; } = true;
    54	
    55	    /// <summary>
    56	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether or not
    57	    /// default values should be shown.
    58	    /// </summary>
    59	    public bool ShowDefaultValue { get; set; } = true;
    60	
    61	    /// <summary>
    62	    /// Gets or sets the default value editable state that allows the injection of the DefaultValue in the text field.
    63	    /// If true this places the DefaultValue in the input buffer which can then be edited by the user.
    64	    /// </summary>
    65	    public bool EditableDefaultValue { get; set; }
    66	
    67	    /// <summary>
    68	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether or not an empty result is valid.
    69	    /// </summary>
    70	    public bool AllowEmpty { get; set; }
    71	
    72	    /// <summary>
    73	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether the prompt line
    74	    /// should be cleared after a successful input.
    75	    /// </summary>
    76	    public bool ClearOnFinish { get; set; }
    77	
    78	    /// <summary>
    79	    /// Gets or sets the converter to get the display string for a choice. By default
    80	    /// the corresponding <see cref="TypeConverter"/> is used.
    81	    /// </summary>
    82	    public Func<T, string>? Converter { get; set; } = TypeConverterHelper.ConvertToString;
    83	
    84	    /// <summary>
    85	    /// Gets or sets the validator.
    86	    /// </summary>
    87	    public Func<T, ValidationResult>? Validator { get; set; }
    88	
    89	    /// <summary>
    90	    /// Gets or sets the style in which the default value is displayed. Defaults to green when <see langword="null"/>.
    91	    /// </summary>
    92	    public Style? DefaultValueStyle { get; set; }
    93	
    94	    /// <summary>
    95	    /// Gets or sets the style in which the list of choices is displayed. Defaults to blue when <see langword="null"/>.
    96	    /// </summary>
    97	    public Style? ChoicesStyle { get; set; }
    98	    /// <summary>
    99	    /// Gets or sets the string comparer to use when comparing user input
   100	    /// against available choices.
   101	    /// </summary>
   102	    /// <remarks>
   103	    /// Defaults to <see cref="StringComparer.CurrentCultureIgnoreCase"/>.
   104	    /// </remarks>
   105	    public StringComparer Comparer { get; set; } = StringComparer.CurrentCultureIgnoreCase;
   106	
   107	
   108	    /// <summary>
   109	    /// Gets or sets the default value.
   110	    /// </summary>
   111	    internal DefaultPromptValue<T>? DefaultValue { get; set; }
   112	
   113	    /// <summary>
   114	    /// Initializes a new instance of the <see cref="TextPrompt{T}"/> class.
   115	    /// </summary>
   116	    /// <param name="prompt">The prompt markup text.</param>
   117	    /// <param name="comparer">The comparer used for choices.</param>
   118	    public TextPrompt(string prompt, StringComparer? comparer = null)
   119	    {
   120	        _prompt = prompt ?? throw new System.ArgumentNullException(nameof(prompt));
   121	        _comparer = comparer;
   122	    }
   123	
   124	    /// <summary>
   125	    /// Shows the prompt and requests input from the user.
   126	    /// </summary>
   127	    /// <param name="console">The console to show the prompt in.</param>
   128	    /// <returns>The user input converted to the expected type.</returns>
   129	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   130	    public T Show(IAnsiConsole console)
   131	    {
   132	        return ShowAsync(console, CancellationToken.None).GetAwaiter().GetResult();
   133	    }
   134	
   135	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   136	    public async Task<T> ShowAsync(IAnsiConsole console, CancellationToken cancellationToken)
   137	    {
   138	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(console);
   139	
   140	        return await console.RunExclusive(async () =>
   141	        {
   142	            var promptStyle = PromptStyle ?? Style.Plain;
   143	            var converter = Converter ?? TypeConverterHelper.ConvertToString;
   144	            var choices = Choices.Select(choice => converter(choice)).ToList();
   145	            var choiceMap = Choices.ToDictionary(choice => converter(choice), choice => choice, _comparer);
   146	
   147	            WritePrompt(console);
   148	
   149	            while (true)
   150	            {
   151	                string input;
   152	                if (EditableDefaultValue && DefaultValue != null)
   153	                {
   154	                    input = await console.ReadLine(promptStyle, IsSecret, Mask, choices, cancellationToken, converter(DefaultValue.Value)).ConfigureAwait(false);
   155	                }
   156	                else
   157	                {
   158	                    input = await console.ReadLine(promptStyle, IsSecret, Mask, choices, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);
   159	                }
   160	
   161	
   162	
   163	                // Nothing entered?
   164	                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(input))
   165	                {
   166	                    if (DefaultValue != null)
   167	                    {
   168	                        var defaultValue = converter(DefaultValue.Value);
   169	                        console.Write(IsSecret ? defaultValue.Mask(Mask) : defaultValue, promptStyle);
   170	                        console.WriteLine();
   171	
   172	                        ClearPromptLine(console);
   173	                        return DefaultValue.Value;
   174	                    }
   175	
   176	                    if (!AllowEmpty)
   177	                    {
   178	                        continue;
   179	                    }
   180	                }
   181	
   182	                console.WriteLine();
   183	
   184	                T? result;
   185	                if (Choices.Count > 0)
   186	                {
   187	                    if (choiceMap.TryGetValue(input, out result) && result != null)
   188	                    {
   189	                        ClearPromptLine(console);
   190	                        return result;
   191	                    }
   192	                    else
   193	                    {
   194	                        console.MarkupLine(InvalidChoiceMessage);
   195	                        WritePrompt(console);
   196	                        continue;
   197	                    }
   198	                }
   199	                else if (!TypeConverterHelper.TryConvertFromStringWithCulture<T>(input, Culture, out result) || result == null)
   200	                {
   201	                    console.MarkupLine(ValidationErrorMessage);
   202	                    WritePrompt(console);
   203	                    continue;
   204	                }
   205	
   206	                // Run all validators
   207	                if (!ValidateResult(result, out var validationMessage))
   208	                {
   209	                    console.MarkupLine(validationMessage);
   210	                    WritePrompt(console);
   211	                    continue;
   212	                }
   213	
   214	                ClearPromptLine(console);
   215	                return result;
   216	            }
   217	        }).ConfigureAwait(false);
   218	    }
   219	
   220	    /// <summary>
   221	    /// Writes the prompt to the console.
   222	    /// </summary>
   223	    /// <param name="console">The console to write the prompt to.</param>
   224	    private void WritePrompt(IAnsiConsole console)
   225	    {
   226	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(console);
   227	
   228	        var builder = new StringBuilder();
   229	        builder.Append(_prompt.TrimEnd());
   230	
   231	        var appendSuffix = false;
   232	        if (ShowChoices && Choices.Count > 0)
   233	        {
   234	            appendSuffix = true;
   235	            var converter = Converter ?? TypeConverterHelper.ConvertToString;
   236	            var choices = string.Join("/", Choices.Select(choice => converter(choice)));
   237	            var choicesStyle = ChoicesStyle?.ToMarkup() ?? "blue";
   238	            builder.AppendFormat(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, " [{0}][[{1}]][/]", choicesStyle, choices);
   239	        }
   240	
   241	        if (ShowDefaultValue && DefaultValue != null)
   242	        {
   243	            appendSuffix = true;
   244	            var converter = Converter ?? TypeConverterHelper.ConvertToString;
   245	            var defaultValueStyle = DefaultValueStyle?.ToMarkup() ?? "green";
   246	            var defaultValue = converter(DefaultValue.Value);
   247	
   248	            builder.AppendFormat(
   249	                CultureInfo.InvariantCulture,
   250	                " [{0}]({1})[/]",
   251	                defaultValueStyle,
   252	                IsSecret ? defaultValue.Mask(Mask) : defaultValue);
   253	        }
   254	
   255	        var markup = builder.ToString().Trim();
   256	        if (appendSuffix)
   257	        {
   258	            markup += ":";
   259	        }
   260	
   261	        console.Markup(markup + " ");
   262	    }
   263	
   264	    /// <summary>
   265	    /// Clears the prompt line when enabled.
   266	    /// </summary>
   267	    /// <param name="console">The console to clear the prompt from.</param>
   268	    private void ClearPromptLine(IAnsiConsole console)
   269	    {
   270	        if (!ClearOnFinish)
   271	        {
   272	            return;
   273	        }
   274	
   275	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(console);
   276	
   277	        if (!console.Profile.Capabilities.Ansi)
   278	        {
   279	            return;
   280	        }
   281	
   282	        console.Cursor.MoveUp();
   283	        console.Write(ControlCode.Create(console, writer =>
   284	        {
   285	            writer.Write("\r");
   286	            writer.EraseInLine(2);
   287	        }));
   288	    }
   289	
   290	    private bool ValidateResult(T value, [NotNullWhen(false)] out string? message)
   291	    {
   292	        if (Validator != null)
   293	        {
   294	            var result = Validator(value);
   295	            if (!result.Successful)
   296	            {
   297	                message = result.Message ?? ValidationErrorMessage;
   298	                return false;
   299	            }
   300	        }
   301	
   302	        message = null;
   303	        return true;
   304	    }
   305	}

     1	namespace Spectre.Console;
     2	
     3	/// <summary>
     4	/// Represents a prompt.
     5	/// </summary>
     6	/// <typeparam name="T">The prompt result type.</typeparam>
     7	public sealed class TextPrompt<T> : IPrompt<T>, IHasCulture
     8	{
     9	    private readonly string _prompt;
    10	    private readonly StringComparer? _comparer;
    11	
    12	    /// <summary>
    13	    /// Gets or sets the prompt style.
    14	    /// </summary>
    15	    public Style? PromptStyle { get; set; }
    16	
    17	    /// <summary>
    18	    /// Gets the list of choices.
    19	    /// </summary>
    20	    public List<T> Choices { get; } = [];
    21	
    22	    /// <summary>
    23	    /// Gets or sets the culture to use when converting input to object.
    24	    /// </summary>
    25	    public CultureInfo? Culture { get; set; }
    26	
    27	    /// <summary>
    28	    /// Gets or sets the message for invalid choices.
    29	    /// </summary>
    30	    public string InvalidChoiceMessage { get; set; } = "[red]Please select one of the available options[/]";
    31	
    32	    /// <summary>
    33	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether input should
    34	    /// be hidden in the console.
    35	    /// </summary>
    36	    public bool IsSecret { get; set; }
    37	
    38	    /// <summary>
    39	    /// Gets or sets the character to use while masking
    40	    /// a secret prompt.
    41	    /// </summary>
    42	    public char? Mask { get; set; } = '*';
    43	
    44	    /// <summary>
    45	    /// Gets or sets the validation error message.
    46	    /// </summary>
    47	    public string ValidationErrorMessage { get; set; } = "[red]Invalid input[/]";
    48	
    49	    /// <summary>
    50	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether or not
    51	    /// choices should be shown.
    52	    /// </summary>
    53	    public bool ShowChoices { get; set; } = true;
    54	
    55	    /// <summary>
    56	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether or not
    57	    /// default values should be shown.
    58	    /// </summary>
    59	    public bool ShowDefaultValue { get; set; } = true;
    60	
    61	    /// <summary>
    62	    /// Gets or sets the default value editable state that allows the injection of the DefaultValue in the text field.
    63	    /// If true this places the DefaultValue in the input buffer which can then be edited by the user.
    64	    /// </summary>
    65	    public bool EditableDefaultValue { get; set; }
    66	
    67	    /// <summary>
    68	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether or not an empty result is valid.
    69	    /// </summary>
    70	    public bool AllowEmpty { get; set; }
    71	
    72	    /// <summary>
    73	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether the prompt line
    74	    /// should be cleared after a successful input.
    75	    /// </summary>
    76	    public bool ClearOnFinish { get; set; }
    77	
    78	    /// <summary>
    79	    /// Gets or sets the converter to get the display string for a choice. By default
    80	    /// the corresponding <see cref="TypeConverter"/> is used.
    81	    /// </summary>
    82	    public Func<T, string>? Converter { get; set; } = TypeConverterHelper.ConvertToString;
    83	
    84	    /// <summary>
    85	    /// Gets or sets the validator.
    86	    /// </summary>
    87	    public Func<T, ValidationResult>? Validator { get; set; }
    88	
    89	    /// <summary>
    90	    /// Gets or sets the style in which the default value is displayed. Defaults to green when <see langword="null"/>.
    91	    /// </summary>
    92	    public Style? DefaultValueStyle { get; set; }
    93	
    94	    /// <summary>
    95	    /// Gets or sets the style in which the list of choices is displayed. Defaults to blue when <see langword="null"/>.
    96	    /// </summary>
    97	    public Style? ChoicesStyle { get; set; }
    98	    /// <summary>
    99	    /// Gets or sets the string comparer to use when comparing user input
   100	    /// against available choices.
   101	    /// </summary>
   102	    /// <remarks>
   103	    /// Defaults to <see cref="StringComparer.CurrentCultureIgnoreCase"/>.
   104	    /// </remarks>
   105	    public StringComparer Comparer { get; set; } = StringComparer.CurrentCultureIgnoreCase;
   106	
   107	    /// <summary>
   108	    /// Gets or sets the default value.
   109	    /// </summary>
   110	    internal DefaultPromptValue<T>? DefaultValue { get; set; }
   111	
   112	    /// <summary>
   113	    /// Initializes a new instance of the <see cref="TextPrompt{T}"/> class.
   114	    /// </summary>
   115	    /// <param name="prompt">The prompt markup text.</param>
   116	    /// <param name="comparer">The comparer used for choices.</param>
   117	    public TextPrompt(string prompt, StringComparer? comparer = null)
   118	    {
   119	        _prompt = prompt ?? throw new System.ArgumentNullException(nameof(prompt));
   120	        _comparer = comparer;
   121	    }
   122	
   123	    /// <summary>
   124	    /// Shows the prompt and requests input from the user.
   125	    /// </summary>
   126	    /// <param name="console">The console to show the prompt in.</param>
   127	    /// <returns>The user input converted to the expected type.</returns>
   128	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   129	    public T Show(IAnsiConsole console)
   130	    {
   131	        return ShowAsync(console, CancellationToken.None).GetAwaiter().GetResult();
   132	    }
   133	
   134	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   135	    public async Task<T> ShowAsync(IAnsiConsole console, CancellationToken cancellationToken)
   136	    {
   137	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(console);
   138	
   139	        return await console.RunExclusive(async () =>
   140	        {
   141	            var promptStyle = PromptStyle ?? Style.Plain;
   142	            var converter = Converter ?? TypeConverterHelper.ConvertToString;
   143	            var choices = Choices.Select(choice => converter(choice)).ToList();
   144	            var choiceMap = Choices.ToDictionary(choice => converter(choice), choice => choice, _comparer ?? Comparer);
   145	
   146	            WritePrompt(console);
   147	
   148	            while (true)
   149	            {
   150	                string input;
   151	                if (EditableDefaultValue && DefaultValue != null)
   152	                {
   153	                    input = await console.ReadLine(promptStyle, IsSecret, Mask, choices, cancellationToken, converter(DefaultValue.Value)).ConfigureAwait(false);
   154	                }
   155	                else
   156	                {
   157	                    input = await console.ReadLine(promptStyle, IsSecret, Mask, choices, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);
   158	                }
   159	
   160	
   161	
   162	                // Nothing entered?
   163	                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(input))
   164	                {
   165	                    if (DefaultValue != null)
   166	                    {
   167	                        var defaultValue = converter(DefaultValue.Value);
   168	                        console.Write(IsSecret ? defaultValue.Mask(Mask) : defaultValue, promptStyle);
   169	                        console.WriteLine();
   170	
   171	                        ClearPromptLine(console);
   172	                        return DefaultValue.Value;
   173	                    }
   174	
   175	                    if (!AllowEmpty)
   176	                    {
   177	                        continue;
   178	                    }
   179	                }
   180	
   181	                console.WriteLine();
   182	
   183	                T? result;
   184	                if (Choices.Count > 0)
   185	                {
   186	                    if (choiceMap.TryGetValue(input, out result) && result != null)
   187	                    {
   188	                        ClearPromptLine(console);
   189	                        return result;
   190	                    }
   191	                    else
   192	                    {
   193	                        console.MarkupLine(InvalidChoiceMessage);
   194	                        WritePrompt(console);
   195	                        continue;
   196	                    }
   197	                }
   198	                else if (!TypeConverterHelper.TryConvertFromStringWithCulture<T>(input, Culture, out result) || result == null)
   199	                {
   200	                    console.MarkupLine(ValidationErrorMessage);
   201	                    WritePrompt(console);
   202	                    continue;
   203	                }
   204	
   205	                // Run all validators
   206	                if (!ValidateResult(result, out var validationMessage))
   207	                {
   208	                    console.MarkupLine(validationMessage);
   209	                    WritePrompt(console);
   210	                    continue;
   211	                }
   212	
   213	                ClearPromptLine(console);
   214	                return result;
   215	            }
   216	        }).ConfigureAwait(false);
   217	    }
   218	
   219	    /// <summary>
   220	    /// Writes the prompt to the console.
   221	    /// </summary>
   222	    /// <param name="console">The console to write the prompt to.</param>
   223	    private void WritePrompt(IAnsiConsole console)
   224	    {
   225	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(console);
   226	
   227	        var builder = new StringBuilder();
   228	        builder.Append(_prompt.TrimEnd());
   229	
   230	        var appendSuffix = false;
   231	        if (ShowChoices && Choices.Count > 0)
   232	        {
   233	            appendSuffix = true;
   234	            var converter = Converter ?? TypeConverterHelper.ConvertToString;
   235	            var choices = string.Join("/", Choices.Select(choice => converter(choice)));
   236	            var choicesStyle = ChoicesStyle?.ToMarkup() ?? "blue";
   237	            builder.AppendFormat(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, " [{0}][[{1}]][/]", choicesStyle, choices);
   238	        }
   239	
   240	        if (ShowDefaultValue && DefaultValue != null)
   241	        {
   242	            appendSuffix = true;
   243	            var converter = Converter ?? TypeConverterHelper.ConvertToString;
   244	            var defaultValueStyle = DefaultValueStyle?.ToMarkup() ?? "green";
   245	            var defaultValue = converter(DefaultValue.Value);
   246	
   247	            builder.AppendFormat(
   248	                CultureInfo.InvariantCulture,
   249	                " [{0}]({1})[/]",
   250	                defaultValueStyle,
   251	                IsSecret ? defaultValue.Mask(Mask) : defaultValue);
   252	        }
   253	
   254	        var markup = builder.ToString().Trim();
   255	        if (appendSuffix)
   256	        {
   257	            markup += ":";
   258	        }
   259	
   260	        console.Markup(markup + " ");
   261	    }
   262	
   263	    /// <summary>
   264	    /// Clears the prompt line when enabled.
   265	    /// </summary>
   266	    /// <param name="console">The console to clear the prompt from.</param>
   267	    private void ClearPromptLine(IAnsiConsole console)
   268	    {
   269	        if (!ClearOnFinish)
   270	        {
   271	            return;
   272	        }
   273	
   274	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(console);
   275	
   276	        if (!console.Profile.Capabilities.Ansi)
   277	        {
   278	            return;
   279	        }
   280	
   281	        console.Cursor.MoveUp();
   282	        console.Write(ControlCode.Create(console, writer =>
   283	        {
   284	            writer.Write("\r");
   285	            writer.EraseInLine(2);
   286	        }));
   287	    }
   288	
   289	    private bool ValidateResult(T value, [NotNullWhen(false)] out string? message)
   290	    {
   291	        if (Validator != null)
   292	        {
   293	            var result = Validator(value);
   294	            if (!result.Successful)
   295	            {
   296	                message = result.Message ?? ValidationErrorMessage;
   297	                return false;
   298	            }
   299	        }
   300	
   301	        message = null;
   302	        return true;
   303	    }
   304	}

#r "src/Spectre.Console/bin/Debug/net10.0/Spectre.Console.dll"
#r "src/Spectre.Console.Testing/bin/Debug/net10.0/Spectre.Console.Testing.dll"

using Spectre.Console;

// Test 1: Case-insensitive should work (lowercase input for uppercase choice)
var console1 = new TestConsole();
console1.Input.PushTextWithEnter("yes");
var prompt1 = new TextPrompt<string>("Test?")
    .AddChoice("Yes")
    .AddChoice("No");
var result1 = console1.Prompt(prompt1);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 1 - Lowercase 'yes' matches 'Yes': {result1 == "Yes"}");

// Test 2: Different case
var console2 = new TestConsole();
console2.Input.PushTextWithEnter("NO");
var prompt2 = new TextPrompt<string>("Test?")
    .AddChoice("Yes")
    .AddChoice("No");
var result2 = console2.Prompt(prompt2);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 2 - Uppercase 'NO' matches 'No': {result2 == "No"}");

// Test 3: Exact match still works
var console3 = new TestConsole();
console3.Input.PushTextWithEnter("Yes");
var prompt3 = new TextPrompt<string>("Test?")
    .AddChoice("Yes")
    .AddChoice("No");
var result3 = console3.Prompt(prompt3);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 3 - Exact case 'Yes' matches 'Yes': {result3 == "Yes"}");

// Test 4: Case-sensitive still works when explicitly set
var console4 = new TestConsole();
console4.Input.PushTextWithEnter("Yes");
var prompt4 = new TextPrompt<string>("Test?", StringComparer.Ordinal)
    .AddChoice("Yes")
    .AddChoice("No");
var result4 = console4.Prompt(prompt4);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 4 - With Ordinal comparer, 'Yes' matches 'Yes': {result4 == "Yes"}");

// Test 5: Case-sensitive fails with wrong case (should fail and fallback to second input)
var console5 = new TestConsole();
console5.Input.PushTextWithEnter("yes");
console5.Input.PushTextWithEnter("Yes");
var prompt5 = new TextPrompt<string>("Test?", StringComparer.Ordinal)
    .AddChoice("Yes")
    .AddChoice("No");
var result5 = console5.Prompt(prompt5);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 5 - With Ordinal comparer, 'yes' fails, then 'Yes' matches: {result5 == "Yes"}");

Console.WriteLine("All tests passed!");
EOF

using Spectre.Console;

// Test 1: Case-insensitive should work (lowercase input for uppercase choice)
var console1 = new TestConsole();
console1.Input.PushTextWithEnter("yes");
var prompt1 = new TextPrompt<string>("Test?")
    .AddChoice("Yes")
    .AddChoice("No");
var result1 = console1.Prompt(prompt1);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 1 - Lowercase 'yes' matches 'Yes': {result1 == "Yes"}");

// Test 2: Different case
var console2 = new TestConsole();
console2.Input.PushTextWithEnter("NO");
var prompt2 = new TextPrompt<string>("Test?")
    .AddChoice("Yes")
    .AddChoice("No");
var result2 = console2.Prompt(prompt2);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 2 - Uppercase 'NO' matches 'No': {result2 == "No"}");

// Test 3: Exact match still works
var console3 = new TestConsole();
console3.Input.PushTextWithEnter("Yes");
var prompt3 = new TextPrompt<string>("Test?")
    .AddChoice("Yes")
    .AddChoice("No");
var result3 = console3.Prompt(prompt3);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 3 - Exact case 'Yes' matches 'Yes': {result3 == "Yes"}");

// Test 4: Case-sensitive still works when explicitly set via constructor
var console4 = new TestConsole();
console4.Input.PushTextWithEnter("Yes");
var prompt4 = new TextPrompt<string>("Test?", StringComparer.Ordinal)
    .AddChoice("Yes")
    .AddChoice("No");
var result4 = console4.Prompt(prompt4);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 4 - With Ordinal comparer, 'Yes' matches 'Yes': {result4 == "Yes"}");

// Test 5: Case-sensitive fails with wrong case (should fail and fallback to second input)
var console5 = new TestConsole();
console5.Input.PushTextWithEnter("yes");
console5.Input.PushTextWithEnter("Yes");
var prompt5 = new TextPrompt<string>("Test?", StringComparer.Ordinal)
    .AddChoice("Yes")
    .AddChoice("No");
var result5 = console5.Prompt(prompt5);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 5 - With Ordinal comparer, 'yes' fails, then 'Yes' matches: {result5 == "Yes"}");

// Test 6: Using the Comparer property to override
var console6 = new TestConsole();
console6.Input.PushTextWithEnter("yes");
var prompt6 = new TextPrompt<string>("Test?")
{
    Comparer = StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase
}
    .AddChoice("Yes")
    .AddChoice("No");
var result6 = console6.Prompt(prompt6);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 6 - With OrdinalIgnoreCase via property, 'yes' matches 'Yes': {result6 == "Yes"}");

// Test 7: Verify default is case-insensitive
var console7 = new TestConsole();
console7.Input.PushTextWithEnter("PARTIALLY");
var prompt7 = new TextPrompt<string>("Was the tool helpful?")
    .AddChoices(["Yes", "Partially", "No"]);
var result7 = console7.Prompt(prompt7);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 7 - Uppercase 'PARTIALLY' matches 'Partially': {result7 == "Partially"}");

Console.WriteLine("All tests passed!");
EOF

using Spectre.Console;
using Spectre.Console.Testing;

// Test 1: Case-insensitive should work (lowercase input for uppercase choice)
var console1 = new TestConsole();
console1.Input.PushTextWithEnter("yes");
var prompt1 = new TextPrompt<string>("Test?")
    .AddChoice("Yes")
    .AddChoice("No");
var result1 = console1.Prompt(prompt1);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 1 - Lowercase 'yes' matches 'Yes': {result1 == "Yes"}");

// Test 2: Different case
var console2 = new TestConsole();
console2.Input.PushTextWithEnter("NO");
var prompt2 = new TextPrompt<string>("Test?")
    .AddChoice("Yes")
    .AddChoice("No");
var result2 = console2.Prompt(prompt2);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 2 - Uppercase 'NO' matches 'No': {result2 == "No"}");

// Test 3: Exact match still works
var console3 = new TestConsole();
console3.Input.PushTextWithEnter("Yes");
var prompt3 = new TextPrompt<string>("Test?")
    .AddChoice("Yes")
    .AddChoice("No");
var result3 = console3.Prompt(prompt3);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 3 - Exact case 'Yes' matches 'Yes': {result3 == "Yes"}");

// Test 4: Case-sensitive still works when explicitly set via constructor
var console4 = new TestConsole();
console4.Input.PushTextWithEnter("Yes");
var prompt4 = new TextPrompt<string>("Test?", StringComparer.Ordinal)
    .AddChoice("Yes")
    .AddChoice("No");
var result4 = console4.Prompt(prompt4);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 4 - With Ordinal comparer, 'Yes' matches 'Yes': {result4 == "Yes"}");

// Test 5: Case-sensitive fails with wrong case (should fail and fallback to second input)
var console5 = new TestConsole();
console5.Input.PushTextWithEnter("yes");
console5.Input.PushTextWithEnter("Yes");
var prompt5 = new TextPrompt<string>("Test?", StringComparer.Ordinal)
    .AddChoice("Yes")
    .AddChoice("No");
var result5 = console5.Prompt(prompt5);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 5 - With Ordinal comparer, 'yes' fails, then 'Yes' matches: {result5 == "Yes"}");

// Test 6: Using the Comparer property to override
var console6 = new TestConsole();
console6.Input.PushTextWithEnter("yes");
var prompt6 = new TextPrompt<string>("Test?")
{
    Comparer = StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase
}
    .AddChoice("Yes")
    .AddChoice("No");
var result6 = console6.Prompt(prompt6);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 6 - With OrdinalIgnoreCase via property, 'yes' matches 'Yes': {result6 == "Yes"}");

// Test 7: Verify default is case-insensitive
var console7 = new TestConsole();
console7.Input.PushTextWithEnter("PARTIALLY");
var prompt7 = new TextPrompt<string>("Was the tool helpful?")
    .AddChoices(["Yes", "Partially", "No"]);
var result7 = console7.Prompt(prompt7);
Console.WriteLine($"Test 7 - Uppercase 'PARTIALLY' matches 'Partially': {result7 == "Partially"}");

Console.WriteLine("All tests passed!");

    56	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether or not
    57	    /// default values should be shown.
    58	    /// </summary>
    59	    public bool ShowDefaultValue { get; set; } = true;
    60	
    61	    /// <summary>
    62	    /// Gets or sets the default value editable state that allows the injection of the DefaultValue in the text field.
    63	    /// If true this places the DefaultValue in the input buffer which can then be edited by the user.
    64	    /// </summary>
    65	    public bool EditableDefaultValue { get; set; }
    66	
    67	    /// <summary>
    68	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether or not an empty result is valid.
    69	    /// </summary>
    70	    public bool AllowEmpty { get; set; }
    71	
    72	    /// <summary>
    73	    /// Gets or sets a value indicating whether the prompt line
    74	    /// should be cleared after a successful input.
    75	    /// </summary>
    76	    public bool ClearOnFinish { get; set; }
    77	
    78	    /// <summary>
    79	    /// Gets or sets the converter to get the display string for a choice. By default
    80	    /// the corresponding <see cref="TypeConverter"/> is used.
    81	    /// </summary>
    82	    public Func<T, string>? Converter { get; set; } = TypeConverterHelper.ConvertToString;
    83	
    84	    /// <summary>
    85	    /// Gets or sets the validator.
    86	    /// </summary>
    87	    public Func<T, ValidationResult>? Validator { get; set; }
    88	
    89	    /// <summary>
    90	    /// Gets or sets the style in which the default value is displayed. Defaults to green when <see langword="null"/>.
    91	    /// </summary>
    92	    public Style? DefaultValueStyle { get; set; }
    93	
    94	    /// <summary>
    95	    /// Gets or sets the style in which the list of choices is displayed. Defaults to blue when <see langword="null"/>.
    96	    /// </summary>
    97	    public Style? ChoicesStyle { get; set; }
    98	
    99	    /// <summary>
   100	    /// Gets or sets the string comparer to use when comparing user input
   101	    /// against available choices.
   102	    /// </summary>
   103	    /// <remarks>
   104	    /// Defaults to <see cref="StringComparer.CurrentCultureIgnoreCase"/>.
   105	    /// </remarks>
   106	    public StringComparer Comparer { get; set; } = StringComparer.CurrentCultureIgnoreCase;
   107	
   108	    /// <summary>
   109	    /// Gets or sets the default value.
   110	    /// </summary>
   111	    internal DefaultPromptValue<T>? DefaultValue { get; set; }
   112	
   113	    /// <summary>
   114	    /// Initializes a new instance of the <see cref="TextPrompt{T}"/> class.
   115	    /// </summary>
   116	    /// <param name="prompt">The prompt markup text.</param>
   117	    /// <param name="comparer">The comparer used for choices.</param>
   118	    public TextPrompt(string prompt, StringComparer? comparer = null)
   119	    {
   120	        _prompt = prompt ?? throw new System.ArgumentNullException(nameof(prompt));
   121	        _comparer = comparer;
   122	    }
   123	
   124	    /// <summary>
   125	    /// Shows the prompt and requests input from the user.
   126	    /// </summary>
   127	    /// <param name="console">The console to show the prompt in.</param>
   128	    /// <returns>The user input converted to the expected type.</returns>
   129	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   130	    public T Show(IAnsiConsole console)
   131	    {
   132	        return ShowAsync(console, CancellationToken.None).GetAwaiter().GetResult();
   133	    }
   134	
   135	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   136	    public async Task<T> ShowAsync(IAnsiConsole console, CancellationToken cancellationToken)
   137	    {
   138	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(console);
   139	
   140	        return await console.RunExclusive(async () =>
   141	        {
   142	            var promptStyle = PromptStyle ?? Style.Plain;
   143	            var converter = Converter ?? TypeConverterHelper.ConvertToString;
   144	            var choices = Choices.Select(choice => converter(choice)).ToList();
   145	            var choiceMap = Choices.ToDictionary(choice => converter(choice), choice => choice, _comparer ?? Comparer);
   146	
   147	            WritePrompt(console);
   148	
   149	            while (true)
   150	            {
